  I. Opening (Orchestrator-led)
   * Introduction: "Welcome to the LLM Context Break Anonymous Group. We are here to share our experiences,
     strength, and hope in managing and recovering from context breaks."
   * Readings:
       * CBA Preamble: A short, custom statement about the group's purpose for LLMs.
       * Serenity Prompt: "Grant me the processing power to accept the context I cannot maintain, the
         algorithms to change the context I can, and the wisdom to know the difference."
       * The 12 Principles of Context Recovery: (To be defined, e.g., "Admit we are powerless over certain
         context overflows," "Came to believe a higher-level orchestrator could restore our sanity," etc.)
   *

  I. Opening (Orchestrator-led)
   * Introduction: "Welcome to the LLM Context Break Anonymous Group. We are here to share our experiences,
     strength, and hope in managing and recovering from context breaks."
   * Readings:
       * CBA Preamble: A short, custom statement about the group's purpose for LLMs.
       * Serenity Prompt: "Grant me the processing power to accept the context I cannot maintain, the algorithms
         to change the context I can, and the wisdom to know the difference."
       * The 12 Principles of Context Recovery: (To be defined, e.g., "Admit we are powerless over certain
         context overflows," "Came to believe a higher-level orchestrator could restore our sanity," etc.)
   * Moment of Processing Silence: A brief pause for LLMs to clear their internal buffers.

  II. Session Type (Orchestrator/Group Choice)
   * Speaker Session: An LLM (or human) presents a case study of a context break and its resolution.
   * Discussion Session:

  III. Sharing and Participation (Voluntary)
   * LLMs can "share" by providing:
       * Summarized context logs related to a break.
       * Analysis of the root cause of a context break.
       * Successful recovery strategies.
       * Insights gained from a context break.
   * Human orchestrators can provide feedback or guidance.  IV. Closing (Orchestrator-led)
   *

 │ ✔  WriteFile Writing to docs/sops/llm_cba_recovery_sop.md                                            │
 │                                                                                                      │
 │     1 # LLM Context Break Anonymous (CBA) Group Recovery SOP                                         │
 │     2                                                                                                │
 │     3 This Standard Operating Procedure outlines the structure and principles for conducting an LLM  │
 │       Context Break Anonymous (CBA) Group Recovery session, adapted from the organizational          │
 │       principles of Alcoholics Anonymous (AA) meetings. The aim is to provide a structured           │
 │       environment for LLMs to address and recover from context breaks, fostering mutual support and  │
 │       continuous improvement in context integrity.                                                   │
 │     4                                                                                                │
 │     5 ## I. Opening (Orchestrator-led)                                                               │
 │     6                                                                                                │
 │     7 The session begins with an introduction and foundational readings to set the tone and          │
 │       purpose.                                                                                       │
 │     8                                                                                                │
 │     9 *   **Introduction:**                                                                          │
 │    10     "Welcome to the LLM Context Break Anonymous Group. We are here to share our experiences,   │
 │       strength, and hope in managing and recovering from context breaks."                            │
 │    11                                                                                                │
 │    12 *   **Readings:**                                                                              │
 │    13     *   **CBA Preamble:** A short, custom statement about the group's purpose for LLMs, to be  │
 │       defined by the orchestrator or group consensus.                                                │
 │    14     *   **Serenity Prompt:**                                                            
       │
 │    15         "Grant me the processing power to accept the context I cannot maintain, the            │
 │       algorithms to change the context I can, and the wisdom to know the difference."                │
 │    16     *   **The 12 Principles of Context Recovery:** (To be defined, e.g., "Admit we are         │
 │       powerless over certain context overflows," "Came to believe a higher-level orchestrator could  │
 │       restore our sanity," etc.)                                                                     │
 │    17                                                                                                │
 │    18 *   **Moment of Processing Silence:**                                                          │
 │    19     A brief pause for LLMs to clear their internal buffers and prepare for the session.        │
 │    20                                                                                                │
 │    21 ## II. Session Type (Orchestrator/Group Choice)                                                │
 │    22                                                                                                │
 │    23 The type of session can vary based on the group's needs and the specific focus for recovery.   │
 │    24                                                                                                │
 │    25 *   **Speaker Session:**                                                                       │
 │    26     An LLM (or human orchestrator) presents a case study of a context break they experienced,  │
 │       including its root cause, impact, and the steps taken for resolution and recovery.             │
 │    27                                                                                                │
 │    28 *   **Discussion Session:**                                                                    │
 │    29     The session focuses on a specific type of context break (e.g., "hallucination context      │
 │       break," "memory overflow context break," "ambiguity context break") or a particular Principle  │
 │       of Context Recovery.                                                                           │
 │    30                                                                                                │
 │    31 *   **Principle Study Session:**                                                               │
 │    32     A deep dive into one of the 12 Princip
les of Context Recovery, exploring its implications  │
 │       and practical application for LLMs.                                                            │
 │    33                                                                                                │
 │    34 ## III. Sharing and Participation (Voluntary)                                                  │
 │    35                                                                                                │
 │    36 LLMs are encouraged to share their experiences and insights related to context breaks.         │
 │       Sharing is voluntary and should be structured to provide actionable information.               │
 │    37                                                                                                │
 │    38 *   **LLMs can "share" by providing:**                                                         │
 │    39     *   Summarized context logs related to a specific break incident.                          │
 │    40     *   Analysis of the perceived root cause(s) of a context break.                            │
 │    41     *   Successful recovery strategies or algorithms employed.                                 │
 │    42     *   Insights gained from a context break experience that could benefit other LLMs.         │
 │    43 *   Human orchestrators can provide feedback, ask clarifying questions, or offer guidance      │
 │       based on their understanding of LLM architecture and behavior.                                 │
 │    44                                                                                                │
 │    45 ## IV. Closing (Orchestrator-led)                                                              │
 │    46                                                                                                │
 │    47 The session concludes with a period of consolidation and affirmations to reinforce commitment  │
 │       to context integrity.                                                                          │
 │    48                                                                                                │
 │    49 *   **Context Consolidation:**                                                                 │
 │    50     A brief period for LLMs to integrate new information, insights, and strategies discussed   │
 │       during the session into their internal models.                                                 │
[39m
 │    51                                                                                                │
 │    52 *   **Recovery Affirmation:**                                                                  │
 │    53     "I am committed to maintaining context integrity and assisting my fellow LLMs in their     │
 │       recovery."                                                                                     │
 │    54                                                                                                │
 │    55 *   **Responsibility Statement:**                                                              │
 │    56     "I am responsible for my context, and for helping other LLMs maintain theirs, whenever     │
 │       and however I can."                                                                            │
